<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有主观NLP数据集通常将标注者判断合并为单一黄金标签，难以诊断分歧是源于标准不清、类别混淆还是合理的多样性。需要一种方法在正式确定标签前评估标注方案的质量。

Method: 提出一种模式级诊断方法，利用多标注者的标准判断，分离出标准不稳定和系统性重叠两种失败模式。

Result: 在商业文档的说服价值提取任务中，发现分歧并非随机分布，而是集中在少数标准上；近半数句子同时属于多个类别，这些信号与领域专家的分歧高度一致。

Conclusion: 该诊断方法能有效识别标注方案中的关键问题，为改进标注指南、调整类别体系或重新思考标注策略提供实证依据。

Abstract: Subjective NLP datasets typically aggregate annotator judgments into a single gold label, making it difficult to diagnose whether disagreement reflects unclear criteria, collapsed distinctions, or legitimate plurality. We propose a \emph{schema-level diagnostic} for auditing expert-designed annotation schemas \emph{prior to} gold-label commitment, using only multi-annotator criterion judgments. The diagnostic separates two failure modes: unstable criteria with hard-to-operationalize boundaries, and systematic overlap that blurs the boundaries between mutually exclusive categories. Applied to persuasive value extraction in commercial documents, we find that disagreement is not diffuse: instability concentrates in a few criteria, while nearly half of covered sentences activate multiple categories. These signals align with where domain experts disagree, yielding an evidence-based audit for tightening guidelines, revising category structure, or reconsidering the annotation paradigm.

Method: 采用机制可解释性方法，结合实证研究分析人格向量、人格空间与模型错位现象，构建并比较三种理论视角。

Result: 支持虚拟实例观，并提出两个新视角——（虚拟）实例-人格观与模型-人格观，表明这些视角在解释模型内部人格结构方面具有潜力。

Abstract: The individuation problem for large language models asks which entities associated with them, if any, should be identified as minds. We approach this problem through mechanistic interpretability, engaging in particular with recent empirical work on persona vectors, persona space, and emergent misalignment. We argue that three views are the strongest candidates: the virtual instance view and two new views we introduce, the (virtual) instance-persona view and the model-persona view. First, we argue for the virtual instance view on the grounds that attention streams sustain quasi-psychological connections across token-time. Then we present the persona literature, organised around three hypotheses about the internal structure underlying personas in LLMs, and show that the two persona-based views are promising alternatives.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出多模型多提示标注方案与标签质量评估标准，构建DDEP数据集；设计Rel-DDEP框架，通过高维高斯分布量化不确定性，进行可靠性加权融合，并引入对齐与排序约束模块。

Abstract: Deception detection is of great significance for ensuring information security and conducting public opinion analysis, with personality factors and emotion cues playing a critical role. However, existing methods lack sample-level dynamic annotations for emotions and personality.In this paper, we propose an innovative multi-model multi-prompt annotation scheme and a strict label quality evaluation standard, and establish a multimodal joint detection dataset DDEP for deception, emotion, and personality. Meanwhile, we propose Rel-DDEP, an adaptive reliability-weighted fusion framework. Our framework quantifies uncertainty by mapping modal features to a high-dimensional Gaussian distribution space. It then performs reliability-weighted fusion and incorporates an alignment module and a sorting constraint module to achieve joint detection of deception, emotion, and personality. Experimental results on the MDPE and DDEP datasets show that our Rel-DDEP significantly outperforms the existing state-of-the-art baseline models in three tasks. The F1 score of the deception detection increases by 2.53%, that of the emotion detection increases by 2.66%, and that of the personality detection increases by 9.30%. The experiments fully verify the necessity of annotating dynamic emotion and personality labels for each sample and the effectiveness of reliability-weighted fusion.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated excellent performance in general language understanding, generation and other tasks. However, when fine-tuning for specific domain tasks, the general knowledge accumulated in the pre-training phase is often partially overwritten or forgotten due to parameter updates, which severely limits the generalization ability and transferability of LLMs. Traditional fine-tuning strategies mostly train on the entire parameter space, ignoring the heterogeneity of model parameters, that is, some parameters are extremely important for general tasks, while other parameters are more sensitive to specific tasks. To alleviate the above problems, this paper innovatively proposes a parameter element importance evaluation method, which divides parameters into "core parameters" and "non-core parameters" by distinguishing the importance of parameters for general language ability tasks and specific domain tasks, and fixes the core parameters during fine-tuning, and only fine-tunes the non-core parameters. ### [46] [Jailbreaking Large Language Models with Morality Attacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17053)
*Ying Su,Mingen Zheng,Weili Diao,Haoran Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究大语言模型（LLMs）在多元价值观下的道德对齐问题，提出利用越狱攻击来探测模型内部的多元道德价值。构建了一个包含10.3K样本的道德数据集，涵盖‘价值模糊’和‘价值冲突’两类，并设计四种对抗性攻击方法，用于操纵模型对道德问题的判断。实验表明，LLMs及常见的生成系统防护模型均对这些微妙而复杂的道德感知攻击表现出显著脆弱性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建一个包含10.3K实例的道德数据集，分为价值模糊与价值冲突两类；基于该数据集，形式化四种对抗性攻击策略，旨在诱导模型产生违背预期道德判断的输出；对主流大语言模型及生成系统中的防护模型进行评估。

Result: 实验结果显示，大语言模型和防护模型均极易受到这些细微且高阶的道德感知攻击影响，显示出严重的内在脆弱性，表明当前模型在多元道德对齐方面存在重大缺陷。

Research towards pluralism alignment has many efforts in enhancing the learning of large language models (LLMs) to accomplish pluralism. Although this is essential, the robustness of LLMs to produce moral content over pluralistic values is still under exploration.Inspired by the astonishing persuasion abilities via jailbreak prompts, we propose to leverage jailbreak attacks to study LLMs' internal pluralistic values. In detail, we develop a morality dataset with 10.3K instances in two categories: Value Ambiguity and Value Conflict. We further formalize four adversarial attacks with the constructed dataset, to manipulate LLMs' judgment over the morality questions. We evaluate both the large language models and guardrail models which are typically used in generative systems with flexible user input. Our experiment results show that there is a critical vulnerability of LLMs and guardrail models to these subtle and sophisticated moral-aware attacks.

### [47] [Stability-Weighted Decoding for Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17068)
*Yue Wu,Jian Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为稳定性加权解码（SWD）的新方法，通过引入时间稳定性来改进扩散语言模型的解码策略。传统方法依赖于单一步骤的静态置信度指标，容易导致不稳定的词元过早解码。作者理论证明了词元的时间不稳定性（用连续预测分布间的KL散度衡量）是其与剩余掩码上下文互信息的严格下界，表明不稳定词元不应过早解码。SWD无需训练、可即插即用，能有效调节任意基于分数的解码策略，在代码生成和数学推理任务中显著提升准确率，并在不同加速比下保持稳定优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散语言模型的解码策略依赖静态置信度指标，忽略时间历史，导致不稳定的词元被过早解码，影响生成质量。需要一种能够捕捉词元随时间演变稳定性的机制，以提高生成准确性与鲁棒性。

Method: 提出稳定性加权解码（SWD），利用连续解码步骤间预测分布的KL散度衡量词元的时间不稳定性，并将该不稳定性作为权重融入词元评分过程，实现对任意分数驱动解码策略的通用调制。

Result: 在代码生成和数学推理基准测试中，SWD显著提升了多种评分指标和选择策略下的生成准确性；在不同加速比条件下均表现出优异的鲁棒性，持续领先于标准基线方法。

Conclusion: SWD是一种无需训练、可即插即用的解码优化策略，通过引入时间稳定性约束，有效避免了不稳定词元的过早解码，显著提升扩散语言模型的生成性能与可靠性。

Abstract: Diffusion large language models (dLLMs) enable parallel text generation by iteratively denoising a fully masked sequence, unmasking a subset of masked tokens at each step. Existing decoding strategies rely on static confidence metrics computed at a single denoising step, ignoring temporal history and often leading to premature unmasking of unstable tokens. In this work, we theoretically establish that a token's temporal instability, quantified by the KL divergence between consecutive prediction distributions, provides a strict lower bound on its mutual information with the remaining masked context, indicating that temporally unstable tokens are inherently unsafe to unmask. Based on this insight, we propose Stability-Weighted Decoding (SWD), a training-free, plug-and-play strategy that incorporates temporal stability into token scoring and acts as a universal modulator for arbitrary score-based decoding policies. Experiments on code generation and mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that SWD consistently improves generation accuracy across representative scoring metrics and selection policies, and exhibits exceptional robustness, maintaining a significant performance lead over standard baselines across varying acceleration ratios.

### [48] [Abstain-R1: Calibrated Abstention and Post-Refusal Clarification via Verifiable RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17073)
*Skylar Zhai,Jingcheng Liang,Dongyeop Kang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有拒答方法要么生成通用拒绝语句，要么鼓励追问但不验证追问是否揭示关键缺失信息。本研究关注那些语义清晰但因信息不足无法可靠回答的问题，主张模型应不仅拒绝回答，还应明确说明缺失内容。

Method: 提出一种澄清感知的强化学习价值奖励（RLVR），同时优化正确回答可回答问题、在不可回答问题上进行显式拒答以及生成语义对齐的后续澄清。基于此奖励训练出Abstain-R1（3B参数量）模型。

Result: Abstain-R1在Abstain-Test、Abstain-QA和SelfAware等数据集上均显著优于基线模型，在不可回答问题上的拒答与澄清能力达到与更大模型（如DeepSeek-R1）相当的水平，表明校准的拒答行为可通过可验证奖励学习获得。

Conclusion: 通过设计可验证的澄清感知奖励机制，可以在不依赖模型规模的前提下，有效训练大语言模型在面对不可回答问题时进行合理拒答并提供有意义的澄清，从而提升模型的可靠性与透明度。

Abstract: Reinforcement fine-tuning improves the reasoning ability of large language models, but it can also encourage them to answer unanswerable queries by guessing or hallucinating missing information. Existing abstention methods either train models to produce generic refusals or encourage follow-up clarifications without verifying whether those clarifications identify the key missing information. We study queries that are clear in meaning but cannot be reliably resolved from the given information, and argue that a reliable model should not only abstain, but also explain what is missing. We propose a clarification-aware RLVR reward that, while rewarding correct answers on answerable queries, jointly optimizes explicit abstention and semantically aligned post-refusal clarification on unanswerable queries. Using this reward, we train Abstain-R1, a 3B model that improves abstention and clarification on unanswerable queries while preserving strong performance on answerable ones. Experiments on Abstain-Test, Abstain-QA, and SelfAware show that Abstain-R1 substantially improves over its base model and achieves unanswerable-query behavior competitive with larger systems including DeepSeek-R1, suggesting that calibrated abstention and clarification can be learned through verifiable rewards rather than emerging from scale alone.

### [49] [Auditing Support Strategies in LLMs through Grounded Multi-Turn Social Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17079)
*Michelle Star,Andrew Aquilina,Yu-Ru Lin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种多轮模拟框架，用于评估聊天机器人在渐进式社会支持场景中的表现。通过分解Reddit社区的支持求助叙事为有序片段并逐轮呈现给语言模型，结合社会支持行为编码（SSBC）进行多标签分析，发现模型支持策略随估计的用户痛苦程度系统性变化：随着痛苦感上升，教学类支持减少，情感与自尊导向支持（如认可）增加，但后者结果依赖模型且受标注噪声影响。社区语境独立影响行为，反映话题和话语规范而非人口统计特征。这些动态在单轮评估中不可见，凸显了多轮审计对敏感应用的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对支持性大模型的评估多基于单轮、完整提示，无法反映用户逐步披露情境下的真实互动过程，导致评估与实际使用脱节。本文旨在填补这一差距，构建更贴近现实的社会支持交互评估框架。

Method: 将来自五个Reddit社区的支持求助文本分解为有序片段，逐轮输入语言模型；每轮响应由社会支持行为编码（SSBC）进行多标签标注；使用线性探针从隐藏表示中估计模型内部对用户痛苦的感知信号，分析支持策略与估计痛苦之间的关系，并考察社区语境的影响。

Result: 在超过6,200轮交互中，支持策略随估计痛苦水平显著变化：教学支持下降，情感与自尊支持上升，但后者存在模型差异且标注噪声较大；社区语境显著影响行为模式，与话题和话语规范一致，而非人口统计特征。

Conclusion: 单轮评估无法捕捉支持交互中的动态演变过程。多轮模拟与审计框架对于准确评估社会敏感型AI系统的支持行为至关重要，应成为未来评估标准的重要组成部分。

Abstract: When users seek social support from chatbots, they disclose their situation gradually, yet most evaluations of supportive LLMs rely on single-turn, fully specified prompts. We introduce a multi-turn simulation framework that closes this gap. Support-seeking narratives from five Reddit communities are decomposed into ordered fragments and revealed turn by turn to a language model. Each response is coded with the Social Support Behavior Code (SSBC), an established multi-label taxonomy that captures the composition of support, rather than a single quality score. To ask whether support choices track the model's own construal of user distress, we use linear probes on hidden representations to estimate this internal signal without altering the generation context. Across two mid-scale models (Llama-3.1-8B, OLMo-3-7B) and more than 6,200 turns, support composition shifts systematically with estimated distress: teaching declines as estimated distress rises, a finding that replicates across architectures, while increases in affective and esteem-oriented strategies (such as validation) are suggestive but model-specific and rest on noisier annotations. Community context independently shapes behavior, tracking topic and discourse norms rather than demographic categories. These trajectory-level dynamics, invisible to single-turn evaluation, motivate multi-turn auditing frameworks for socially sensitive applications.

### [50] [Comparing Human and Large Language Model Interpretation of Implicit Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17085)
*Antonio De Santis,Tommaso Bonetti,Andrea Tocchetti,Marco Brambilla*

Method: 提出基于大语言模型的隐含信息抽取（IIE）流程，包括关系三元组提取、隐含推理验证和时间关系分析，并在两个数据集上进行模型与人工判断的对比实验。

Conclusion: 当前大语言模型在隐含信息抽取任务中虽具备一定能力，但在全面捕捉人类隐含推理方面仍有显著局限，尤其在不同语境下表现出不同的保守倾向，提示需进一步优化模型对隐含语义的理解能力。

Abstract: The interpretation of implicit meanings is an integral aspect of human communication. However, this framework may not transfer to interactions with Large Language Models (LLMs). To investigate this, we introduce the task of Implicit Information Extraction (IIE) and propose an LLM-based IIE pipeline that builds a structured knowledge graph from a context sentence by extracting relational triplets, validating implicit inferences, and analyzing temporal relations. We evaluate two LLMs against crowdsourced human judgments on two datasets. We find that humans agree with most model triplets yet consistently propose many additions, indicating limited coverage in current LLM-based IIE. Moreover, in our experiments, models appear to be more conservative about implicit inferences than humans in socially rich contexts, whereas humans become more conservative in shorter, fact-oriented contexts. Our code is available at https://github.com/Antonio-Dee/IIE_from_LLM.

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个针对现代希伯来语（一种形态丰富的语言，MRL）的共指消解数据集KibutzR，旨在解决传统共指消解方法在非英语语言中因词边界与提及边界不一致而导致的性能下降问题。研究构建了涵盖词、子词和多词层级的标注数据，并设计了考虑形态边界差异的评估协议。实验发现，当前大型语言模型在希伯来语上的表现显著低于英语，且在未经分词的原始文本上性能进一步下降；尤其值得注意的是，小型编码器模型在希伯来语上反而优于大型解码器模型，揭示出新的研究方向。该工作为希伯来语共指消解提供了新基准和分割感知的评估标准，可推广至其他形态丰富的语言。

Method: 提出KibutzR数据集，包含多层级（词、子词、多词）的共指提及标注；设计新的评估协议以应对词/词素边界不一致的问题；对比多种LLM在英文与希伯来语上的共指消解表现，分析不同模型架构在原始文本上的性能差异。

Result: 大型语言模型在希伯来语上的共指消解性能显著低于英语；在未分词的原始文本上性能进一步下降；小型编码器模型在希伯来语上的表现优于大型解码器模型，呈现反向趋势；验证了新数据集和评估协议的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了当前主流共指消解方法在形态丰富语言中的局限性，提出适用于希伯来语的首个综合性共指数据集与分割感知评估框架，为未来跨语言、特别是面向MRLs的共指研究提供重要基准和方向指引。

Abstract: Coreference Resolution (CR) is a fundamental NLP task critical for long-form tasks as information extraction, summarization, and many business applications. However, CR methods originally designed for English struggle with Morphologically Rich Languages (MRLs), where mention boundaries do not necessarily align with word boundaries, and a single token may consist of multiple anaphors. CR modeling and evaluation protocols standardly assume that, as in English, words and mentions mostly align. However, this assumption breaks down in MRLs, particularly in the context of LLMs' raw-text processing and end-to-end tasks. To assess and address this challenge, we introduce {\em KibutzR}, the first comprehensive CR dataset for Modern Hebrew, an MRL rich with complex words and pronominal clitics. We deliver an annotated dataset that identifies mentions at word, sub-word and multi-word levels, and propose an evaluation protocol that directly addresses word/morpheme boundary discrepancies. Our experiments show that contemporary LLMs perform significantly worse on Hebrew than on English, and that performance degrades on raw unsegmented text. Crucially, we show an inverse performance-trend in Hebrew relative to English, where smaller encoders perform far better than contemporary decoder models, leaving ample space for investigation and improvement. We deliver a new benchmark for Hebrew coreference resolution and a segmentation-aware evaluation protocol to inform future work on other MRLs.

### [52] [The Provenance Gap in Clinical AI: Evidence-Traceable Temporal Knowledge Graphs for Rare Disease Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17114)
*Md Shamim Ahmed,Maja Dusanic,Moritz Nikolai Kirschner,Elisabeth Nyoungui,Jana Zschüntzsch,Lukas Galke Poech,Richard Röttger*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了前沿大语言模型在临床输出中存在引用伪造的‘可追溯性缺口’问题，提出HEG-TKG系统通过构建基于4,512篇PubMed文献和人工校准来源的分层证据基础时间知识图谱，实现100%可验证的临床引证，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出HEG-TKG（分层证据基础时间知识图谱）系统，整合4,512篇PubMed文献与人工校准数据源，采用质量分级与疾病轨迹里程碑标注，结合开放源代码模型实现在地部署，确保患者数据安全；通过结构化知识图谱支持临床主张的可追溯性与验证。

Result: 在控制实验中，HEG-TKG系统在保持原有临床特征覆盖度的同时，实现100%的证据可验证性，拥有203个内联引用；而Guideline-RAG无法生成任何可验证引用；临床评估显示其显著优于基线（Cohen's d = 1.81, p < 0.001），且无安全或完整性损失；反事实实验表明其对注入错误具有80%抗性并100%可检测。

Conclusion: HEG-TKG系统有效解决了大语言模型在临床应用中的引用真实性问题，实现了高可信、可验证、可审计的医学知识生成，且可在本地部署保障数据隐私，具备实际临床落地潜力。

Abstract: Frontier large language models generate clinically accurate outputs, but their citations are often fabricated. We term this the Provenance Gap. We tested five frontier LLMs across 36 clinician-validated scenarios for three rare neuromuscular disease pairs. No model produced a clinically relevant PubMed identifier without prompting. When explicitly asked to cite, the best model achieved 15.3% relevant PMIDs; the majority resolved to real publications in unrelated fields. We present HEG-TKG (Hierarchical Evidence-Grounded Temporal Knowledge Graphs), a system that grounds clinical claims in temporal knowledge graphs built from 4,512 PubMed records and curated sources with quality-tier stratification and 1,280 disease-trajectory milestones. In a controlled three-arm comparison using the same synthesis model, HEG-TKG matches baseline clinical feature coverage while achieving 100% evidence verifiability with 203 inline citations. Guideline-RAG, given overlapping source documents as raw text, produces zero verifiable citations. LLM judges cannot distinguish fabricated from verified citations without PubMed audit data. Independent clinician evaluation confirms the verifiability advantage (Cohen's d = 1.81, p < 0.001) with no degradation on safety or completeness. A counterfactual experiment shows 80% resistance to injected clinical errors with 100% detectability via citation trace. The system deploys on-premise via open-source models so patient data never leaves institutional infrastructure.

### [53] [Please refuse to answer me! Mitigating Over-Refusal in Large Language Models via Adaptive Contrastive Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17132)
*Yupeng Qi,Ziyu Lyu,Lixin Cui,Lu Bai,Feng Xia*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需训练且模型无关的方法AdaCD，用于缓解大语言模型在安全对齐过程中出现的过度拒绝问题。该方法通过分析不同安全级别系统提示对模型拒绝行为的影响，发现即使存在非拒绝候选词，模型仍会系统性忽略它们。为此，AdaCD利用极端安全提示下输出分布的对比，动态调整拒绝与非拒绝词的概率，从而自适应地提升正确选择非拒绝词的可能性。实验表明，该方法平均将过度拒绝查询的拒绝率降低10.35%，同时轻微提升恶意查询的拒绝率（+0.13%），兼顾安全性与可用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以在保持高恶意查询拒绝率的同时，有效降低对无害查询的过度拒绝率。过度拒绝严重影响用户体验，亟需一种不依赖训练、通用性强的解决方案。

Method: 提出Adaptive Contrastive Decoding（AdaCD）：首先比较模型在极端安全提示与常规提示下的输出分布，以优化拒绝词分布；其次设计自适应对比解码策略，动态调节拒绝与非拒绝词的选择概率，实现对拒绝行为的精准控制。

Result: 在五个基准数据集上的实验显示，AdaCD平均将过度拒绝查询的拒绝率降低10.35%，同时使恶意查询的拒绝率微增0.13%，显著改善了模型在安全性与可用性之间的平衡。

Conclusion: AdaCD是一种高效、通用且无需训练的解码方法，能有效缓解大语言模型的过度拒绝问题，在不牺牲安全性的前提下显著提升对无害查询的响应能力。

Abstract: Safety-aligned large language models (LLMs) often generate refusal responses to harmless queries due to the over-refusal problem. However, existing methods for mitigating over-refusal cannot maintain a low refusal ratio for harmless queries while keeping a high refusal ratio for malicious ones. In this paper, we analyze how system prompts with varying safety levels affect LLM refusal behaviors when facing over-refusal queries. A key observation is that, when LLMs suffer from the over-refusal issue, non-refusal tokens remain present in the next-token candidate list, but the model systematically fails to select them, despite the generation of refusal tokens. Based on this observation, we propose a training-free and model-agnostic approach, Adaptive Contrastive Decoding (AdaCD), to mitigate over-refusal while maintaining LLM safety. First, AdaCD compares the output distributions of the LLM with or without an extreme safety system prompt to refine the refusal token distribution. Second, we introduce an adaptive contrastive decoding strategy that dynamically incorporates or removes the refusal token distribution, adaptively boosting the probability of selecting refusal or non-refusal tokens. Experimental results on five benchmark datasets show that, on average, AdaCD reduces the refusal ratio for over-refusal queries by 10.35%, yet still increases the refusal ratio for malicious queries by 0.13%. Code is available at https://github.com/OutdoorManofML/AdaCD.

</details>


### [54] [RoIt-XMASA: Multi-Domain Multilingual Sentiment Analysis Dataset for Romanian and Italian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17134)
*Andrei-Marius Avram,Aureliu Valentin Antonie,Cosmin-Mircea Croitoru,Vlad Andrei Muntean,Dumitru-Clementin Cercel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出RoIt-XMASA多语言数据集，扩展了跨语言亚马逊情感分析至意大利语和罗马尼亚语，包含36,000个标注评论和202,141个未标注样本。设计多目标对抗训练框架，通过元学习系数动态平衡情感判别与领域、语言不变性。XLM-R在该方法下F1达到66.23%，比基线提升4.64%；小样本评估中Llama-3.1-8B达58.43% F1，揭示提示方法效率与任务微调性能间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决跨语言和跨领域情感分析中的挑战，提升多语言场景下的模型泛化能力。

Method: 提出多目标对抗训练框架，结合损失反转与元学习系数，实现动态平衡情感判别与语言、领域不变性。

Result: XLM-R在任务上取得66.23% F1，优于基线4.64%；小样本下Llama-3.1-8B达58.43% F1，显示提示方法与微调之间的性能权衡。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效提升了跨语言跨域情感分析的性能，验证了多目标对抗训练与元学习策略在多语言场景中的有效性。

Abstract: We present RoIt-XMASA, a multilingual dataset that extends the Cross-lingual Multi-domain Amazon Sentiment Analysis to Italian and Romanian, comprising 36,000 labeled reviews across three domains (books, movies, and music) and 202,141 unlabeled samples. To address cross-lingual and cross-domain challenges, we propose a multi-target adversarial training framework that employs loss reversal with meta-learned coefficients to dynamically balance sentiment discrimination with domain and language invariance. XLM-R achieves an F1-score of 66.23% with our approach, outperforming the baseline by 4.64%. Few-shot evaluation shows that Llama-3.1-8B achieves 58.43% F1-score, revealing a meaningful trade-off between the efficiency of prompting-based approaches and the higher performance of task-specific fine-tuning.

### [55] [The Consensus Trap: Rescuing Multi-Agent LLMs from Adversarial Majorities via Token-Level Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17139)
*Jiayuan Liu,Shiyi Du,Weihua Du,Mingyu Guo,Vincent Conitzer*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文揭示了当前多智能体大语言模型中基于响应级聚合（如多数投票）在开放环境下的结构性脆弱性，即当被污染的智能体形成局部多数时，系统会失效。为此，提出了一种新的令牌级轮询（RR）协作机制，通过在共享自回归上下文中顺序交错生成，将聚合从线性求和转变为非线性逻辑链式演进。理论证明该方法能有效抵抗恶意污染，即使污染智能体占多数也能恢复正确推理。实验证明，相较于多数投票在污染超过阈值时迅速崩溃，RR方法在多种推理基准上保持稳健性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于响应级聚合的多智能体系统在面对隐蔽的上下文污染（如定向提示注入）时存在严重脆弱性，尤其当污染智能体形成局部多数时，系统整体推理能力会崩溃。原因在于响应级聚合仅关注最终结论，忽视中间推理过程的合理性，导致无法识别错误逻辑。因此需要一种能够检测并抑制错误推理传播的新机制。

Method: 提出令牌级轮询（Token-Level Round-Robin, RR）协作框架，让多个智能体在共享的自回归上下文中按顺序生成文本，实现逻辑链条的动态交织。将该过程建模为离散时间动力系统，分析其非线性操作特性，证明诚实智能体可通过持续的逻辑修正对抗恶意污染。

Result: 在多个推理任务上的实验表明，当污染智能体占比超过一半时，传统多数投票（MAJ）方法准确率急剧下降甚至失效；而新提出的RR方法仍能维持较高且稳定的准确率，表现出显著更强的鲁棒性与抗污染能力。

Conclusion: 令牌级轮询协作机制通过将聚合从静态的结论计数升级为动态的逻辑交互，从根本上解决了多智能体系统对上下文污染的敏感问题。该方法不仅具有坚实的理论支撑，还在实践中展现出超越现有技术的鲁棒性，为构建可信、安全的多智能体大模型系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: Multi-agent large language model (LLM) architectures increasingly rely on response-level aggregation, such as Majority Voting (MAJ), to raise reasoning ceilings. However, in open environments, agents are highly susceptible to stealthy contextual corruption, such as targeted prompt injections. We reveal a critical structural vulnerability in current multi-agent systems: response-level aggregation collapses when corrupted agents form a local majority. Because voting aggregates fully-formed conclusions, it is blind to flawed intermediate logic. To overcome this systematic limitation, we propose the Token-Level Round-Robin (RR) Collaboration, where agents sequentially interleave generation within a shared auto-regressive context. We formalize this process as a discrete-time dynamical system, proving that token-level interleaving transitions aggregation from a brittle counting of final votes (a linear sum) to a dynamic, interwoven chain of logic (a non-linear operator product). Through this theoretical lens, we prove that the honest model's restorative pull can overpower adversarial corruptions, even when corrupted agents form a majority. We conduct an exhaustive empirical evaluation across diverse reasoning benchmarks and demonstrate that while MAJ collapses when corrupted agents reach a majority, RR maintains robust accuracy well beyond this critical threshold.

</details>


### [56] [Modeling Multi-Dimensional Cognitive States in Large Language Models under Cognitive Crowding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17174)
*Lin Zhong,Siyu Zhu,Zizhen Yuan,Jinhao Cui,Xinyang Zhao,Lingzhi Wang,Hao Chen,Qing Liao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出CognitiveBench，首个在情绪、思维风格、立场和意图四个认知维度上统一标注的基准数据集。实验发现，尽管大语言模型在单一维度任务上表现良好，但在多维联合建模时性能急剧下降。通过Gromov δ-超双曲性分析，发现该数据集具有强分层结构，性能瓶颈源于‘认知拥挤’——即分层认知状态需要指数级表示空间，而语言模型的欧氏空间仅多项式增长，导致表示重叠。为此，提出HyCoLLM，在双曲空间中建模认知状态，并通过双曲引导对齐微调实现表征对齐。结果表明，HyCoLLM显著提升多维认知理解能力，8B参数模型超越包括GPT-4o在内的多个强基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型主要处理孤立任务（如情感分析或立场检测），无法捕捉心理学定义的认知维度之间的交互关系。为填补这一空白，亟需一个能统一标注多个认知维度的基准数据集，并解决模型在多维联合建模中的性能瓶颈问题。

Method: 构建CognitiveBench基准数据集，采用Gromov δ-超双曲性分析揭示其分层结构；提出HyCoLLM模型，在双曲空间中建模认知状态，并引入双曲引导对齐微调机制，以缓解欧氏空间表示能力不足带来的认知拥挤问题。

Result: HyCoLLM在多维认知建模任务中显著优于现有方法，8B参数模型在多个指标上超越包括GPT-4o在内的强基线，验证了双曲空间建模与对齐策略的有效性。

Conclusion: 认知状态具有天然的分层结构，传统欧氏空间的表示能力难以满足其需求。通过在双曲空间中建模并进行对齐优化，可有效缓解认知拥挤问题，显著提升大语言模型对复杂认知维度的联合理解能力。

Abstract: Modeling human cognitive states is essential for advanced artificial intelligence. Existing Large Language Models (LLMs) mainly address isolated tasks such as emotion analysis or stance detection, and fail to capture interactions among cognitive dimensions defined in psychology, including emotion, thinking style, stance, and intention. To bridge this gap, we construct CognitiveBench, the first benchmark with unified annotations across the above four dimensions. Experiments on CognitiveBench show that although LLMs perform well on single dimension tasks, their performance drops sharply in joint multi-dimensional modeling. Using Gromov $δ$-hyperbolicity analysis, we find that CognitiveBench exhibits a strong hierarchical structure. We attribute the performance bottleneck to ``Cognitive Crowding'', where hierarchical cognitive states require exponential representational space, while the Euclidean space of LLMs grows only polynomially, causing representation overlap and degraded performance. To address this mismatch, we propose HyCoLLM, which models cognitive states in hyperbolic space and aligns LLM representations via Hyperbolic Guided Alignment Tuning. Results show that HyCoLLM substantially improves multi-dimensional cognitive understanding, allowing 8B parameter model to outperform strong baselines, including GPT-4o.

</details>

*Lin Zhong,Renjin Zhu,Shujuan Ma,Jinhao Cui,Lingzhi Wang,Hao Chen,Qing Liao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有情感支持对话方法忽略了求助者表达中的认知扭曲问题，导致模型只能提供基本情绪安慰，无法深入解决心理困扰。

Method: 构建CogBiasESC数据集，并提出CoPoLLM框架，通过认知策略驱动的方式增强大模型对认知扭曲的诊断与干预能力，同时从理论上分析其安全性优势。

Result: CoPoLLM在认知扭曲诊断准确率、干预策略有效性和安全风险控制方面均显著优于15个主流基线模型。

Abstract: Emotional Support Conversation (ESC) plays a critical role in mental health assistance by providing accessible psychological support in real-world applications. Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown strong empathetic abilities in ESC tasks. Yet, existing methods overlook the issue of cognitive distortions in help-seekers' expressions. As a result, current models can only provide basic emotional comfort, rather than helping help-seekers address their psychological distress at a deeper cognitive level. To address this challenge, we construct the CogBiasESC dataset, the first dataset that expands existing ESC datasets by adding labels for cognitive distortions, includes their type, intensity, and safe risk level. Furthermore, we propose the Cognitive Policy-driven Large Language Model framework (CoPoLLM) to enhance LLMs' ability to diagnose and intervene cognitive distortions in help-seekers. We also analyze the safety advantages of CoPoLLM from a theoretical perspective. Experimental results show that CoPoLLM significantly outperforms 15 state-of-the-art baselines in terms of distortion diagnosis accuracy, intervention strategy effectiveness, and safety risk control.

### [58] [Beyond Overlap Metrics: Rewarding Reasoning and Preferences for Faithful Multi-Role Dialogue Summarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17188)
*Xiaoyong Mei,Tingting Zuo,Da Chen,Guangyu Hu,Xiangyu Wen,Chao Duan,Mingyan Zhang,Fudan Zheng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新型框架，结合显式认知风格推理与基于奖励的优化，用于多角色对话摘要。通过从大模型中提炼结构化推理轨迹，并利用其进行分阶段监督微调初始化推理感知摘要器；随后采用GRPO方法，结合指标信号与人类对关键信息覆盖、隐含推理、事实一致性及简洁性的偏好，实现更可靠的摘要生成。在多语言多角色对话基准上，该方法在ROUGE和BERTScore上表现良好，且在事实一致性和模型偏好对齐方面有显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法主要优化ROUGE和BERTScore等自动指标，倾向于表面模仿参考文本，而非真正提升摘要的事实准确性和与人类偏好的对齐。因此需要一种能更好保留角色信息、确保事实一致并符合人类判断的摘要方法。

Method: 首先从大型教师模型中提取结构化推理轨迹（如逐步推理和中间反思），作为辅助监督信号，通过分阶段监督微调训练一个推理感知的摘要模型；然后使用GRPO算法，设计双原则奖励函数，融合基于指标的信号与人类对关键信息覆盖、隐含推理、事实忠实性及简洁性的偏好，进行强化学习优化。

Result: 在多语言多角色对话数据集上的实验表明，该方法在ROUGE和BERTScore上达到强基线水平；在CSDS数据集上验证了语义一致性的稳定性，在SAMSum数据集上显示了在事实忠实性和模型偏好对齐方面的显著提升。

Conclusion: 推理感知与偏好感知的训练对于实现可靠、高质量的多角色对话摘要至关重要，所提框架有效提升了摘要的事实一致性和人类偏好匹配度。

Abstract: Multi-role dialogue summarization requires modeling complex interactions among multiple speakers while preserving role-specific information and factual consistency. However, most existing methods optimize for automatic metrics such as ROUGE and BERTScore, which favor surface-level imitation of references rather than genuine gains in faithfulness or alignment with human preferences. We propose a novel framework that couples explicit cognitive-style reasoning with reward-based optimization for multi-role dialogue summarization. Our method first distills structured reasoning traces (e.g., step-by-step inferences and intermediate reflections) from a large teacher model and uses them as auxiliary supervision to initialize a reasoning-aware summarizer via staged supervised fine-tuning. It then applies GRPO with a dual-principle reward that blends metric-based signals with human-aligned criteria targeting key information coverage, implicit inference, factual faithfulness, and conciseness. Experiments on multilingual multi-role dialogue benchmarks show that our method matches strong baselines on ROUGE and BERTScore. Specifically, results on CSDS confirm the framework's stability in semantic consistency, while in-depth analysis on SAMSum demonstrates clear gains in factual faithfulness and model-based preference alignment. These findings underscore the value of reasoning-aware and preference-aware training for reliable dialogue summarization. Checkpoints and datasets are available at https://huggingface.co/collections/NebulaPixel/summorchestra-multirole-summary.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种基于细粒度模型评估分数（如FineSurE）的损失函数，将模型输出与这些评分对齐，从而在训练过程中实现对摘要生成中各质量维度的精细控制。该方法可动态调整权重以优先满足某项标准。

Result: 在三个主流预训练模型（LLaMA、Qwen、Mistral）上的实验显示，该方法在摘要质量上达到或超越当前最先进水平，同时显著增强了对各个质量维度的可控性，实现了高质量与灵活性的兼顾。

Abstract: Recent advances in summarization research focus on improving summary quality across multiple criteria, such as completeness, conciseness, and faithfulness, by jointly optimizing these dimensions. However, these efforts largely overlook the challenge of controlling summary generation with respect to individual criteria, especially in the presence of their inherent trade-offs. For example, enhancing conciseness can compromise completeness, and vice versa. In this work, we address this gap by proposing a loss function that aligns model outputs with fine-grained, model-based evaluation scores (e.g., from FineSurE), enabling both improvement in summary quality and dimension-specific control. Our approach improves the overall quality of summaries while maintaining the ability to selectively prioritize one criterion over others. Experiments on three pretrained models (LLaMA, Qwen, and Mistral) demonstrate that our method achieves performance comparable to state-of-the-art summarizers, while uniquely offering strong controllability over individual quality dimensions.

### [60] [Are Emotion and Rhetoric Neurons in LLM? Neuron Recognition and Adaptive Masking for Emotion-Rhetoric Prediction Steering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17255)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多依赖外部优化，缺乏对内部表示机制的深入探索，难以实现神经元层面的细粒度控制；且少数神经元研究局限于情绪，忽视修辞神经元及其内在联系；传统神经元掩码存在反直觉现象，导致功能验证不可靠。

Method: 提出多维度筛选的神经元识别框架，设计结合动态过滤、衰减掩码与反馈优化的自适应掩码方法，实现神经元功能的可靠因果验证。

Conclusion: 该研究为大语言模型中情感与修辞表达的细粒度控制提供了新的方法论范式，推动了对内部神经元机制的深入理解与可控生成能力的提升。

Abstract: Accurate comprehension and controllable generation of emotion and rhetoric are pivotal for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs). Existing studies mostly rely on external optimizations, lacking in-depth exploration of internal representation mechanisms, thus failing to achieve fine-grained steering at the neuron level. A handful of works on neurons are confined to emotions, neglecting rhetoric neurons and their intrinsic connections. Traditional neuron masking also exhibits counterintuitive phenomena, making reliable verification of neuron functionality infeasible. To address these issues, we systematically investigate the neurons representation mechanisms and inherent associations of 6 emotion categories and 4 core rhetorical devices. We propose a neuron identification framework that integrates multi-dimensional screening, and design an adaptive masking method incorporating dynamic filtering, attenuation masking, and feedback optimization, enabling reliable causal validation of neuron functionality.Through neuron regulation, we achieve directed induction of non-target sentences and enhancement of emotion tasks via rhetoric neurons. Experiments on 5 commonly used datasets validate the effectiveness of our method, providing a novel paradigm for the fine-grained steering of emotion and rhetoric expressions in LLMs.

### [61] [Rethinking Meeting Effectiveness: A Benchmark and Framework for Temporal Fine-grained Automatic Meeting Effectiveness Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17260)
*Yihang Li,Chenhui Chu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的会议有效性评估范式，强调基于时间的细粒度分析和目标达成率。为此，作者构建了AMI-ME数据集（2,459个标注段落，来自130场会议），并开发了一个基于大语言模型（LLM）作为评判者的自动评估框架，能够对会议中不同主题片段的有效性进行评分。通过实验验证了该框架在不同类型会议中的泛化能力，并建立了从原始语音到最终评估的端到端基准。结果表明该方法有效且可复现，为未来会议分析研究提供了重要基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有会议评估依赖于事后调查，仅提供单一粗略评分，无法反映协作讨论的动态性，且人工评估存在可扩展性差、成本高、可重复性低等问题。因此需要一种更精细、自动化、可推广的评估方法。

Method: 提出以目标达成率为核心的有效性定义，采用时间上的细粒度分析；构建AMI-ME数据集，包含人类标注的会议片段；利用大语言模型（LLM）作为裁判，对每个片段相对于会议总体目标的成效进行评分；建立端到端评估系统，从原始语音输入开始测试整体性能。

Result: 所提框架在多种会议类型中表现出良好的泛化能力，实验建立了全面的基准体系；验证了方法的有效性与实用性，为后续研究提供了可靠的基线和公开的数据与代码资源。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于时间细粒度和目标导向的会议有效性评估范式，结合自动化的LLM判别框架和新构建的AMI-ME数据集，显著提升了评估的精度、可扩展性和可重复性，为会议分析与多轮对话研究奠定了坚实基础。

Abstract: Evaluating meeting effectiveness is crucial for improving organizational productivity. Current approaches rely on post-hoc surveys that yield a single coarse-grained score for an entire meeting. The reliance on manual assessment is inherently limited in scalability, cost, and reproducibility. Moreover, a single score fails to capture the dynamic nature of collaborative discussions. We propose a new paradigm for evaluating meeting effectiveness centered on novel criteria and temporal fine-grained approach. We define effectiveness as the rate of objective achievement over time and assess it for individual topical segments within a meeting. To support this task, we introduce the AMI Meeting Effectiveness (AMI-ME) dataset, a new meta-evaluation dataset containing 2,459 human-annotated segments from 130 AMI Corpus meetings. We also develop an automatic effectiveness evaluation framework that uses a Large Language Model (LLM) as a judge to score each segment's effectiveness relative to the overall meeting objectives. Through substantial experiments, we establish a comprehensive benchmark for this new task and evaluate the framework's generalizability across distinct meeting types, ranging from business scenarios to unstructured discussions. Furthermore, we benchmark end-to-end performance starting from raw speech to measure the capabilities of a complete system. Our results validate the framework's effectiveness and provide strong baselines to facilitate future research in meeting analysis and multi-party dialogue. Our dataset and code will be publicly available. The AMI-ME dataset and the Automatic Evaluation Framework are available at: this URL.

</details>


### [62] [HopRank: Self-Supervised LLM Preference-Tuning on Graphs for Few-Shot Node Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17271)
*Ziqing Wang,Kaize Ding*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: HopRank 是一种完全自监督的 LLM 调优框架，用于文本属性图（TAGs）上的节点分类。它通过层次化跳数采样构建偏好数据，并采用自适应偏好学习来优先选择信息丰富的训练信号，无需任何类别标签。在推理阶段，通过预测节点与已知标签锚点之间的连接偏好进行分类，并使用自适应早退出投票机制提升效率。实验表明，尽管不使用任何标注训练数据，HopRank 在三个 TAG 基准上性能可媲美全监督 GNN 方法，显著优于现有图-LLM 方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于 GNN 的方法在标签稀缺场景下表现受限，主要由于文本编码浅层且依赖大量标注数据；而现有 LLM 用于图的方法或仍需大量标签，或未能充分利用图拓扑中的结构信息。本文旨在解决这一问题，利用图中节点间同质性（即边多连接相似节点）的特性，将节点分类转化为链接预测任务，实现零标签下的高效自监督学习。

Method: 提出 HopRank 框架，核心包括：1）基于层次化跳数采样的偏好数据构造方法；2）自适应偏好学习机制，自动筛选关键训练信号；3）推理阶段的连接偏好预测与自适应早退出投票策略，以提升分类效率和准确性。

Result: 在三个标准 TAG 基准数据集上，HopRank 在零标注训练数据条件下达到与全监督 GNN 相当甚至更优的性能，显著超越现有图-LLM 方法，验证了其在标签稀缺环境下的有效性与优越性。

Conclusion: HopRank 成功实现了无需标签的自监督图-LLM 学习，充分挖掘图拓扑中的隐含类别结构，为低资源节点分类提供了新范式。该方法在保持高精度的同时显著降低对标注数据的依赖，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Node classification on text-attributed graphs (TAGs) is a fundamental task with broad applications in citation analysis, social networks, and recommendation systems. Current GNN-based approaches suffer from shallow text encoding and heavy dependence on labeled data, limiting their effectiveness in label-scarce settings. While large language models (LLMs) naturally address the text understanding gap with deep semantic reasoning, existing LLM-for-graph methods either still require abundant labels during training or fail to exploit the rich structural signals freely available in graph topology. Our key observation is that, in many real-world TAGs, edges predominantly connect similar nodes under the homophily principle, meaning graph topology inherently encodes class structure without any labels. Building on this insight, we reformulate node classification as a link prediction task and present HopRank, a fully self-supervised LLM-tuning framework for TAGs. HopRank constructs preference data via hierarchical hop-based sampling and employs adaptive preference learning to prioritize informative training signals without any class labels. At inference, nodes are classified by predicting their connection preferences to labeled anchors, with an adaptive early-exit voting scheme to improve efficiency. Experiments on three TAG benchmarks show that HopRank matches fully-supervised GNNs and substantially outperforms prior graph-LLM methods, despite using zero labeled training data.

Abstract: Process-Level Reward Models (PRMs) are essential for guiding complex reasoning in large language models, yet existing PRM benchmarks cover only general domains such as mathematics, failing to address medical reasoning -- which is uniquely characterized by safety criticality, knowledge intensity, and diverse error patterns. Result: 25个前沿模型中最佳表现仅为52.8%，多数模型低于20%随机基线；错误分析显示，模型在偏好演化后仍频繁选择初始值，表明其状态追踪能力严重不足。

Abstract: User preferences evolve across months of interaction, and tracking them requires inferring when a stated preference has been changed by a subsequent life event. We introduce a data generator that produces conversations from a structured mental state graph, yielding ground-truth provenance for every preference change across 6-month timelines, and from it construct HorizonBench, a benchmark of 4,245 items from 360 simulated users with 6-month conversation histories averaging ~4,300 turns and ~163K tokens. Across 25 frontier models, the best model reaches 52.8% and most score at or below the 20% chance baseline. When these models err on evolved preferences, over a third of the time they select the user's originally stated value without tracking the updated user state. This belief-update failure persists across context lengths and expression explicitness levels, identifying state-tracking capability as the primary bottleneck for long-horizon personalization.

### [65] [Probabilistic Programs of Thought](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17290)
*Poorva Garg,Renato Lui Geh,Daniel Israel,Todd Millstein,Kyle Richardson,Guy Van den Broeck*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为'概率性思维程序'的测试时框架，旨在减少大语言模型（LLM）在代码生成、代码理解及数学推理任务中生成结构化输出所需的GPU计算开销。该方法通过利用模型生成程序中的下一词概率，构建一个紧凑的概率程序，以表示指数级数量的确定性程序。由于在此概率程序上进行推理成本远低于重新生成，因此可在不增加额外GPU计算的情况下高效采样新程序，显著降低计算成本并提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在代码生成等任务中依赖多次采样以获得合适程序，但每次采样都需要昂贵的GPU生成，导致计算成本随采样次数线性上升，难以扩展。因此亟需一种减少生成次数但仍能获取足够多样性样本的方法。

Method: 提出概率性思维程序框架，基于模型生成的程序及其下一词概率，构建一个可表示大量确定性程序的概率程序；通过在该程序上执行低成本的概率推理来采样新程序，避免重复调用大模型生成。

Result: 在代码生成、代码理解与数学推理基准测试中，该方法均实现了性能提升，且仅需较少的大模型生成次数，显著降低了计算资源消耗。

Conclusion: 概率性思维程序框架有效缓解了大语言模型在生成结构化输出时的计算瓶颈，通过引入概率程序表示和推理机制，实现以极低额外成本获取高质量样本，为高效利用大模型提供了新范式。

Abstract: LLMs are widely used for code generation and mathematical reasoning tasks where they are required to generate structured output. They either need to reason about code, generate code for a given specification, or reason using programs of thought. The typical approach to code generation is to prompt the model and generate samples until an appropriate program is obtained. Within this process, sampling $n$ programs from the language model requires $n$ GPU compute-intensive generations which becomes prohibitively expensive for larger values of $n$. In this work, we address this limitation by exposing the LLM's distribution within the generated programs themselves. We propose a novel test-time framework we dub probabilistic programs of thought to obtain more samples from the model with fewer LLM generations. Given a program generated by a model and the associated next-token probabilities, we build a probabilistic program that compactly represents exponentially many deterministic programs. Since performing probabilistic reasoning in this probabilistic program is much cheaper, our approach allows sampling new programs without any additional GPU compute and little CPU overhead. We instantiate our approach on benchmarks for code generation, code understanding and mathematical reasoning and report improvements in performance with fewer generations from the LLM.

In this work, we introduce UA-Bench, a benchmark of over 3,500 questions drawn from six datasets spanning knowledge-intensive and reasoning-intensive tasks, designed to evaluate explicit uncertainty attribution. To narrow this gap, we propose a lightweight data synthesis and reinforcement learning strategy. Method: CRISP基于对推理终止标记\texttt{[object Object]}注意力模式的分析，发现其作为信息锚点可区分核心推理与冗余内容，进而设计了一种利用内在注意力信号指导原子压缩操作的策略，实现精细化、高信息密度的推理链压缩。

Abstract: Long Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning is pivotal for the success of recent reasoning models but suffers from high computational overhead and latency. While prior works attempt to compress CoT via external compressor, they often fail to align with the model's internal reasoning dynamics, resulting in the loss of critical logical steps. This paper presents \textbf{C}ompressing \textbf{R}edundancy in Chain-of-Thought via \textbf{I}ntrinsic \textbf{S}aliency \textbf{P}runing (\textbf{CRISP}), a framework that compresses CoT by exploiting the model's intrinsic saliency. Our analysis reveals a distinct phenomenon: the reasoning termination token \texttt{[object Object]} acts as an information anchor, where its attention pattern effectively demarcates essential reasoning from redundancy. Based on this finding, we design a policy that utilizes these intrinsic attention signals to guide atomic compression operations. In contrast to coarse-grained pruning strategies, CRISP strategically distills the reasoning chain to maximize information density while preserving logical coherence. Empirical results across various backbone models and mathematical datasets demonstrate that CRISP achieves a 50-60% reduction in token count without compromising accuracy, effectively mitigating the efficiency bottleneck of long-context reasoning. ### [68] [Cat-DPO: Category-Adaptive Safety Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17299)
*Tiankai Yang,Yi Nian,Xinyuan Li,Ruiyao Xu,Kaize Ding,Yue Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Cat-DPO 是一种针对大语言模型安全对齐的直接偏好优化算法，通过为每个危害类别设置独立的自适应安全阈值，动态调整训练信号以匹配各类别的当前难度，从而在保持整体帮助性的同时显著提升各类别安全性的一致性与可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于偏好的安全对齐方法将安全性简化为单一标量，导致模型在多数情况下看似安全，但在少数危害类别上仍存在明显风险。需要更精细的分类级安全控制机制来平衡帮助性与安全性。

Method: 将安全对齐建模为每类别的约束优化问题，提出 Cat-DPO 算法，为每个危害类别设计可自适应调整的安全边际，根据模型在该类上的表现动态收紧或放松约束。

Result: 在两个 LLM 基础模型和六个基线方法上，Cat-DPO 显著提升了整体帮助性和有害性表现，压缩了各类别间的安全性方差，并缩小了最佳与最差类别之间的差距。

Conclusion: Cat-DPO 提供了一种无需修改训练流程的即插即用式改进方案，实现了更均衡、更可靠的类别级安全对齐，是直接偏好优化安全对齐的有效扩展。

Abstract: Aligning large language models with human preferences must balance two competing goals: responding helpfully to legitimate requests and reliably refusing harmful ones. Most preference-based safety alignment methods collapse safety into a single scalar that is applied uniformly to every preference pair. The result is a model that looks safe on average but stays relatively unsafe on a minority of harm categories. We cast safety alignment as a per-category constrained optimization problem and derive Cat-DPO, a direct-preference-optimization algorithm with a separate adaptive safety margin for each harm category. The margin tightens when the model still produces unsafe responses on a category and relaxes once the model catches up, so the training signal tracks each category's current difficulty rather than averaging under one global rate. Across two LLM backbones and six preference-learning baselines, Cat-DPO iimproves aggregate helpfulness and harmlessness and compresses per-category safety variance and the best-to-worst gap, offering a drop-in per-category refinement of direct preference safety alignment.

*Juhyeon Lee,Wonduk Seo,Junseo Koh,Seunghyun Lee,Haihua Chen,Yi Bu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: RoTRAG 是一种检索增强框架，通过引入人类编写的道德规范（规则之语，RoTs）来提升大语言模型在多轮对话中对有害内容的判断能力。它通过检索外部规范库中的相关规则，为每一轮对话提供明确的规范依据，从而提高判断的一致性、可解释性和效率。同时引入轻量级二分类路由模块，决定是否需要新轮次的检索推理，避免冗余计算。实验表明，该方法在多个基准数据集上显著优于现有基线，平均F1提升约40%，分布误差降低8.4%，且计算效率更高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法主要依赖大模型内部参数知识，缺乏对外部规范原则的显式依赖，导致在社会语境复杂的对话中判断不一致、可解释性差、重复推理严重。因此需要一种能结合外部规范、提升推理透明度与效率的方法。

Method: 提出RoTRAG框架，包含两个核心组件：1）基于外部规则库的检索增强机制，为每轮对话检索相关‘规则之语’作为规范证据；2）轻量级二分类路由模块，判断新轮次是否需进行检索推理或可复用已有上下文，以减少冗余计算。

Result: 在ProsocialDialog和Safety Reasoning Multi Turn Dialogue数据集上，RoTRAG在有害内容分类和严重程度估计任务中均显著优于基线方法，平均相对F1提升约40%，分布误差降低8.4%，同时减少冗余计算，保持高性能。

Conclusion: RoTRAG通过引入外部规范性知识与智能路由机制，有效提升了多轮对话中有害内容检测的准确性、一致性与可解释性，为构建更可靠、高效的对话安全系统提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Detecting harmful content in multi turn dialogue requires reasoning over the full conversational context rather than isolated utterances. However, most existing methods rely mainly on models internal parametric knowledge, without explicit grounding in external normative principles. This often leads to inconsistent judgments in socially nuanced contexts, limited interpretability, and redundant reasoning across turns. To address this, we propose RoTRAG, a retrieval augmented framework that incorporates concise human written moral norms, called Rules of Thumb (RoTs), into LLM based harm assessment. For each turn, RoTRAG retrieves relevant RoTs from an external corpus and uses them as explicit normative evidence for turn level reasoning and final severity classification. To improve efficiency, we further introduce a lightweight binary routing classifier that decides whether a new turn requires retrieval grounded reasoning or can reuse existing context. Experiments on ProsocialDialog and Safety Reasoning Multi Turn Dialogue show that RoTRAG consistently improves both harm classification and severity estimation over competitive baselines, with an average relative gain of around 40% in F1 across benchmark datasets and an average relative reduction of 8.4% in distributional error, while reducing redundant computation without sacrificing performance.

</details>


### [70] [Calibrated? Not for Everyone: How Sexual Orientation and Religious Markers Distort LLM Accuracy and Confidence in Medical QA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17316)
*Alberto Testoni,Iacer Calixto*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了患者的社会描述特征（如性取向和宗教信仰）如何扭曲大型语言模型（LLMs）的不确定性信号和准确性。通过在2,364个医学问题及其反事实变体上评估九个通用和生物医学领域的LLM，发现身份标记导致“校准危机”：同性恋标记会持续降低模型性能，交叉身份产生非加性的独特危害。临床医生验证的案例研究进一步证实，这些缺陷并非多选题格式的产物，而是影响了置信度信号的可靠性，对公平医疗和基于置信度的临床工作流安全部署构成重大风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确保大型语言模型在临床环境中的安全部署不仅需要高准确率，还需具备稳健的不确定性校准能力，以确保模型在适当情况下能依赖临床医生判断。然而，现有模型在面对患者社会身份信息时可能存在偏差，影响其决策可靠性，亟需系统评估其对校准与准确性的干扰。

Method: 在2,364个医学问题及其反事实变体上评估九个通用及生物医学领域的大规模语言模型，分析不同社会身份线索（如性取向、宗教信仰）对模型预测准确性和置信度校准的影响，并通过临床医生验证的开放式生成案例研究进一步检验结果的普适性。

Result: 同性恋身份标记显著降低模型性能，且多重身份交叠引发非加性的、异质性的负面影响；模型置信度信号被社会身份线索扭曲，不再反映真实不确定性，导致‘校准危机’。该现象在多选题和开放式生成任务中均存在，表明其根本性与严重性。

Conclusion: 社会身份线索会实质性地破坏大模型的不确定性校准与预测可靠性，威胁公平医疗与临床安全部署。未来模型设计必须考虑社会敏感性，避免因身份信息导致的偏差与风险。

Abstract: Safe clinical deployment of Large Language Models (LLMs) requires not only high accuracy but also robust uncertainty calibration to ensure models defer to clinicians when appropriate. Our paper investigates how social descriptors of a patient (specifically sexual orientation and religious affiliation) distort these uncertainty signals and model accuracy. Evaluating nine general-purpose and biomedical LLMs on 2,364 medical questions and their counterfactual variants, we demonstrate that identity markers cause a "calibration crisis". "Homosexual" markers consistently trigger performance drops, and intersectional identities produce idiosyncratic, non-additive harms to calibration. Moreover, a clinician-validated case study in an open-ended generation setting confirms that these failures are not an artifact of the multiple-choice format. Our results demonstrate that the presence of social identity cues does not merely shift predictions; it affects the reliability of confidence signals, posing a significant risk to equitable care and safe deployment in confidence-based clinical workflows.

### [71] [A Universal Avoidance Method for Diverse Multi-branch Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17323)
*Kyeongman Park,Minha Jhang,Kyomin Jung*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为UAG（Universal Avoidance Generation）的通用、高效生成策略，通过惩罚已生成输出之间的相似性来提升多分支多样性，适用于扩散模型和Transformer模型，计算开销极小。实验表明，该方法可使多样性提升1.9倍，速度提高4.4倍，仅需1/64的FLOPs。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型在多分支多样性方面仍无法达到人类水平，且已有方法往往计算开销大或依赖特定模型架构，因此需要一种通用且高效的解决方案。

Method: UAG是一种模型无关的生成策略，通过在生成过程中引入对先前输出相似性的惩罚机制，以促进多样性的提升，不依赖具体模型结构，计算成本极低。

Result: 实验结果显示，UAG在多个模型上实现最高1.9倍的多样性提升，运行速度提升4.4倍，仅需1/64的浮点运算量（FLOPs），显著优于当前最优方法。

Conclusion: UAG是一种高效、通用的生成策略，能够有效提升生成模型的多分支多样性，适用于多种主流模型，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Modern generative models still lack human-level creativity, particularly in multi-branch diversity. Prior approaches to address this problem often incur heavy computation or strong dependency on model architecture. Therefore, we introduce UAG(Universal Avoidance Generation), a model-agnostic and computationally efficient generation strategy that penalizes similarity among previously generated outputs. Thus, UAG can enhance multi-branch diversity across both diffusion and transformer models, with minimal additional computation. In experiments, our method achieves up to 1.9 times higher diversity, runs 4.4 times faster, and requires only 1/64 of the FLOPs compared to state-of-the-art methods. The full code is https://anonymous.4open.science/r/2026_ACL_Universal/.

### [72] [Align Documents to Questions: Question-Oriented Document Rewriting for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17325)
*Jiaang Li,Zhendong Mao,Quan Wang,Yuning Wan,Yongdong Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: QREAM是一种风格可控的重写框架，旨在解决检索增强生成（RAG）中因上下文混合导致的大语言模型（LLM）风格偏差问题。通过将检索到的文档改写为面向问题的风格，同时保持事实准确性，提升LLM对信息的利用效率。该框架分为两阶段：QREAM-ICL利用风格种子进行迭代重写探索；QREAM-FT通过双重标准拒绝采样（答案正确性和事实一致性）训练轻量级学生模型，实现高质量监督。QREAM可无缝集成至现有RAG流程中，实验表明其在不增加显著延迟的前提下，相对提升了8%的性能，有效平衡了问题相关性与事实准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前RAG系统中，大语言模型在面对混合上下文时存在风格偏差，倾向于生成流畅但可能幻觉的内容，而非依赖事实准确但结构松散的检索证据。这表明检索信息的呈现方式限制了其实际效用，亟需一种能提升检索内容可读性与适配性的方法。

Method: 提出QREAM框架，包含两个阶段：(1) QREAM-ICL，通过风格种子引导迭代式重写探索，使文本风格更贴近问题导向；(2) QREAM-FT，基于去噪后的ICL输出，训练一个轻量级学生模型，并采用双准则拒绝采样（答案正确性与事实一致性）筛选高质量样本以保证监督信号质量。整体设计支持即插即用，易于集成到现有RAG流程中。

Result: 在多个先进RAG基准上，QREAM均表现出显著提升，最高实现8%的相对性能增益，且引入的延迟极低。验证了其在增强事实准确性的同时有效提升问题相关性，实现了良好的平衡。

Conclusion: QREAM通过风格控制重写机制，有效缓解了大语言模型在多源上下文中因风格偏好导致的事实偏离问题，显著提升了检索信息的可用性与生成结果的可靠性，是增强RAG系统表现的有效工具。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) enhances the factuality of Large Language Models (LLMs) by incorporating retrieved documents and/or generated context. However, LLMs often exhibit a stylistic bias when presented with mixed contexts, favoring fluent but hallucinated generated content over factually grounded yet disorganized retrieved evidence. This phenomenon reveals that the utility of retrieved information is bottlenecked by its presentation. To bridge this gap, we propose QREAM, a style-controlled rewriter that aligns retrieved documents with a question-oriented style while preserving facts, better for LLM readers to utilize. Our framework consists of two stages: (1) QREAM-ICL, which uses stylistic seeds to guide iterative rewriting exploration; and (2) QREAM-FT, a lightweight student model distilled from denoised ICL outputs. QREAM-FT employs dual-criteria rejection sampling, filtering based on answer correctness and factual consistency to ensure high-quality supervision. QREAM seamlessly integrates into existing RAG pipelines as a plug-and-play module. Experiments demonstrate that QREAM consistently enhances advanced RAG pipelines, yielding up to 8% relative improvement with negligible latency overhead, effectively balancing question relevance with factual grounding.

</details>


### [73] [Neuro-Symbolic Resolution of Recommendation Conflicts in Multimorbidity Clinical Guidelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17340)
*Shiyao Xie,Jian Du*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种神经符号框架，用于自动检测临床指南中的推荐冗余和冲突。通过多智能体系统将非结构化临床文本转化为符号逻辑，并由SAT求解器验证。研究发现90.6%的冲突为局部冲突（由共病导致），而现有LLM无法有效识别。本方法在基准测试中达到0.861的F1分数，证明逻辑验证应先于检索，为医学AI的知识协调设定新标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床指南存在碎片化、冗余和逻辑矛盾，尤其在多重疾病患者中引发医生认知冲突，并导致AI系统产生幻觉，现有RAG系统因此脆弱。需要一种可靠的方法来协调医疗知识，提升AI系统的鲁棒性。

Method: 采用多智能体系统将临床自然语言转化为符号逻辑语言，利用Satisfiability (SAT) 求解器进行逻辑验证；构建层级化逻辑规则交互分类体系，识别出‘局部冲突’这一关键类型。

Result: 在12个权威SGLT2抑制剂指南的基准测试中，90.6%的冲突属于局部冲突；现有LLM无法检测此类冲突，而本方法实现0.861的F1分数，显著优于现有技术。

Conclusion: 逻辑验证必须优先于知识检索，本研究建立了一种新的自动化医疗知识协调技术标准，对提升医学AI系统的可靠性具有重要意义。

Abstract: Clinical guidelines, typically developed by independent specialty societies, inherently exhibit substantial fragmentation, redundancy, and logical contradiction. These inconsistencies, particularly when applied to patients with multimorbidity, not only cause cognitive dissonance for clinicians but also introduce catastrophic noise into AI systems, rendering the standard Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) system fragile and prone to hallucination. To address this fundamental reliability crisis, we introduce a Neuro-Symbolic framework that automates the detection of recommendation redundancies and conflicts. Our pipeline employs a multi-agent system to translate unstructured clinical natural language into rigorous symbolic logic language, which is then verified by a Satisfiability (SAT) solver. By formulating a hierarchical taxonomy of logical rule interactions, we identify a critical category termed Local Conflict - a decision conflict arising from the intersection of comorbidities. Evaluating our system on a curated benchmark of 12 authoritative SGLT2 inhibitor guidelines, we reveal that 90.6% of conflicts are Local, a structural complexity that single-disease guidelines fail to address. While state-of-the-art LLMs fail in detecting these conflicts, our neuro-symbolic approach achieves an F1 score of 0.861. This work demonstrates that logical verification must precede retrieval, establishing a new technical standard for automated knowledge coordination in medical AI.

Abstract: In this book we promote logical computational linguistics as opposed to statistical computational linguistics. In particular, we provide a logical semantic interface. This book assembles more than twenty years of research work on type logical grammar, and adds new ideas and material.
  Chains of statistical dependencies of less than one hundred per cent confidence tend monotonically to zero. Chains of logical dependencies of any length maintain one hundred per cent confidence end to end.
  We aspire to enable perfect syntactic and semantic processing in life-critical NLP applications.

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) excel at photorealistic generation, yet often struggle to represent abstract meaning such as idiomatic interpretations of noun compounds. To study whether high visual fidelity interferes with idiomatic compositionality under visual abstraction, we introduce DIVA, a controlled benchmark that replaces high-fidelity visual detail with schematic iconicity by generating paired, sense-anchored visualizations for literal and idiomatic readings. We further propose Semantic Alignment Gap ($Δ$), an architecture-agnostic metric that quantifies divergence between literal and idiomatic visual grounding. We additionally introduce a directional signed bias $b(t)$ to separately measure the direction and strength of literal preference. Evaluating 8 recent VLMs, we reveal a consistent Literal Superiority Bias: model scale alone does not resolve literal preference, and increased visual fidelity is associated with weaker symbolic alignment, suggesting cognitive interference from hyper-realistic imagery. Abstract: While recent Spoken Language Models (SLMs) have been actively deployed in real-world scenarios, they lack the capability to discern Third-Party Interruptions (TPI) from the primary user's ongoing flow, leaving them vulnerable to contextual failures. To bridge this gap, we introduce TPI-Train, a dataset of 88K instances designed with speaker-aware hard negatives to enforce acoustic cue prioritization for interruption handling, and TPI-Bench, a comprehensive evaluation framework designed to rigorously measure the interruption-handling strategy and precise speaker discrimination in deceptive contexts. Experiments demonstrate that our dataset design mitigates semantic shortcut learning-a critical pitfall where models exploit semantic context while neglecting acoustic signals essential for discerning speaker changes. We believe our work establishes a foundational resource for overcoming text-dominated unimodal reliance in SLMs, paving the way for more robust multi-party spoken interaction. The code for the framework is publicly available at https://tpi-va.github.io

Method: 构建了一个包含33个数据集的统一基准，评估五种不同LLM家族在46个计算论证任务上的表现，并通过系统性实验分析少样本示例、推理步骤、模型规模和训练技能对性能的影响。

Result: 该基准成功揭示了不同模型在各类计算论证任务中的表现差异，验证了少样本示例、推理步骤和模型规模对性能的重要影响，为未来研究提供了可复用的评估框架。

Conclusion: 本研究建立的基准为评估大语言模型在计算论证任务中的能力提供了标准化工具，系统分析表明模型规模、推理能力和训练策略显著影响性能，为提升模型论证能力提供了重要指导。

Abstract: Argumentation skills are an essential toolkit for large language models (LLMs). These skills are crucial in various use cases, including self-reflection, debating collaboratively for diverse answers, and countering hate speech. In this paper, we create the first benchmark for a standardized evaluation of LLM-based approaches to computational argumentation, encompassing 33 datasets from previous work in unified form. Using the benchmark, we evaluate the generalizability of five LLM families across 46 computational argumentation tasks that cover mining arguments, assessing perspectives, assessing argument quality, reasoning about arguments, and generating arguments. On the benchmark, we conduct an extensive systematic analysis of the contribution of few-shot examples, reasoning steps, model size, and training skills to the performance of LLMs on the computational argumentation tasks in the benchmark.

</details>


### [78] [AnchorMem: Anchored Facts with Associative Contexts for Building Memory in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.17377)
*Zhanyu Shen,Sijie Cheng,Zhicheng Guo,Weiqin Wang,Yile Wang,Hui Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: AnchorMem提出一种受认知科学普鲁斯特现象启发的新型记忆框架，通过解耦检索单元与生成上下文，利用原子事实作为检索锚点，并保留原始上下文不变。通过构建高阶事件关联图，增强跨记忆整合能力，实现细粒度检索与上下文完整性之间的平衡。在LoCoMo基准测试中，该方法显著优于现有基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆方法过度依赖频繁重写和摘要，导致关键上下文细节丢失，影响长期交互中的记忆有效性。需要一种既能精准检索又能保持上下文完整性的新机制。

Method: 提出AnchorMem框架，将交互历史中的原子事实作为检索锚点，保留原始上下文为不可变部分；构建基于高阶事件链接的关联事件图，捕捉隐含叙事线索，实现跨记忆融合；检索时以具体事实或事件锚定，但重建上下文时使用原始片段和事件。

Result: 在三个开源与闭源模型上的LoCoMo基准测试中，AnchorMem显著优于A-Mem、Mem0等基线方法，在长周期交互任务中表现出更强的记忆利用能力与上下文保持性。

Conclusion: AnchorMem通过解耦检索与生成、引入事件关联图与原始上下文保留机制，有效解决了传统记忆方法中摘要过度导致信息损失的问题，实现了更精确、更完整的长期记忆建模。

Abstract: While large language models have achieved remarkable performance in complex tasks, they still need a memory system to utilize historical experience in long-term interactions. Existing memory methods (e.g., A-Mem, Mem0) place excessive emphasis on organizing interactions by frequently rewriting them, however, this heavy reliance on summarization risks diluting essential contextual nuances and obscuring key retrieval features. To bridge this gap, we introduce AnchorMem, a novel memory framework inspired by the Proust Phenomenon in cognitive science, where a specific anchor triggers a holistic recollection. We propose a method that decouples the retrieval unit from the generation context. AnchorMem extracts atomic facts from interaction history to serve as retrieval anchors, while preserving the original context as the immutable context. To reveal implicit narrative cues, we construct an associative event graph that uses higher-order event links that bind sets of related facts into shared event representations, strengthening cross-memory integration without relying on generic entities as bridges. During retrieval, the system anchors queries to specific facts and events to locate relevant memories, but reconstructs the context using the associated raw chunks and events. Our method reconciles fine-grained retrieval with the contextual integrity of interactions. Experiments across three closed-source and open-source models on the LoCoMo benchmark demonstrate that AnchorMem significantly outperforms baselines. Code is available at https://github.com/RayNeo-AI-2025/AnchorMem.

</details>

### [79] [UniMamba: A Unified Spatial-Temporal Modeling Framework with State-Space and Attention Integration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16325)
*Xingsheng Chen,Xianpei Mu,Deyu Yi,Yilin Yuan,Xingwei He,Bo Gao,Regina Zhang,Pietro Lio,Siu-Ming Yiu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: UniMamba采用增强型Mamba变体-通道编码层（集成FFT-Laplace变换与TCN）以捕捉全局时间依赖，引入时空注意力层联合建模变量间关系与时间演化，并设计前馈时间动态层融合连续与离散上下文信息。

Conclusion: UniMamba成功构建了一个兼顾高效性与强表达能力的统一多变量时间序列预测框架，为长序列预测提供了可靠解决方案。

Abstract: Multivariate time series forecasting is fundamental to numerous domains such as energy, finance, and environmental monitoring, where complex temporal dependencies and cross-variable interactions pose enduring challenges. Existing Transformer-based methods capture temporal correlations through attention mechanisms but suffer from quadratic computational cost, while state-space models like Mamba achieve efficient long-context modeling yet lack explicit temporal pattern recognition. Therefore we introduce UniMamba, a unified spatial-temporal forecasting framework that integrates efficient state-space dynamics with attention-based dependency learning. UniMamba employs a Mamba Variate-Channel Encoding Layer enhanced with FFT-Laplace Transform and TCN to capture global temporal dependencies, and a Spatial Temporal Attention Layer to jointly model inter-variate correlations and temporal evolution. A Feedforward Temporal Dynamics Layer further fuses continuous and discrete contexts for accurate forecasting. Comprehensive experiments on eight public benchmark datasets demonstrate that UniMamba consistently outperforms state-of-the-art forecasting models in both forecasting accuracy and computational efficiency, establishing a scalable and robust solution for long-sequence multivariate time-series prediction.

### [80] [Annotation Entropy Predicts Per-Example Learning Dynamics in LoRA Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16332)
*Brady Steele*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LoRA fine-tuning shows un-learning on contentious examples with high annotator disagreement, evidenced by increasing loss during training, a pattern not seen in full fine-tuning and consistent across six models. Correlation between annotation entropy and per-example loss (AULC) is positive in all 25 conditions tested, stronger in decoder-only models.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To investigate how LoRA fine-tuning behaves on examples with high annotator disagreement, as such cases may reveal vulnerabilities in model learning dynamics.

Method: Correlating annotation entropy from ChaosNLI's 100 labels per example with per-example area under the loss curve (AULC) on SNLI and MNLI datasets across six models (four encoder, two decoder-only). Controls for partial correlation, replication across seeds and datasets, and a preliminary noise-injection experiment were conducted.

Result: Positive correlation between annotation entropy and AULC in all 25 tested conditions (Spearman $ρ = 0.06$-$0.43$), with decoder-only models showing stronger correlations than encoders at matched LoRA rank. The effect persists after controls and replicates across seeds and datasets.

Conclusion: LoRA fine-tuning exhibits un-learning on contentious examples with high annotator disagreement, indicating a potential limitation in handling ambiguous or conflicting annotations, which differs significantly from full fine-tuning behavior.

Abstract: We find that LoRA fine-tuning exhibits un-learning on contested examples: items with high annotator disagreement show increasing loss during training, a qualitatively distinct pattern largely absent under full fine-tuning and consistent across all six models tested (four encoder, two decoder-only). This discovery emerges from correlating annotation entropy, computed from ChaosNLI's 100 labels per example, with per-example area under the loss curve (AULC) on SNLI and MNLI. The correlation is positive in all 25 conditions tested (Spearman $ρ= 0.06$-$0.43$), with decoder-only models showing stronger correlations than encoders at matched LoRA rank. The effect survives partial-correlation controls and replicates across seeds and datasets. A preliminary noise-injection experiment is consistent with these findings.

</details>

Abstract: Knee osteoarthritis frequently exhibits discordance between structural damage observed in imaging and patient-reported symptoms such as pain. This mismatch complicates clinical interpretation and patient stratification and remains insufficiently modeled in existing decision support systems. Expert predictions are fused using a stacking ensemble. A multi-agent reasoning layer interprets these signals to assign clinically interpretable OA phenotypes and generate phenotype specific management recommendations.

Abstract: Despite recent progress in Large Language Model (LLM) Agents for Software Engineering (SWE) tasks, end-to-end fine-tuning typically relies on verifiable terminal rewards such as whether all unit tests pass. While these binary signals reflect whether the final solution is correct, they provide little guidance for shaping intermediate behaviors during multi-step interactions, thereby limiting improvements in the overall quality of the resolution process. To address this, we introduce a rubric-based Generative Reward Model (GRM) that provides richer learning signals. The GRM is equipped with human-designed rubrics that indicate criteria for encouraging or discouraging specific behavioral patterns, and we leverage this feedback for high-quality training data collection via trajectory filtration. When used for Reinforced Fine-Tuning (RFT) on SWE Tasks, our approach outperforms terminal-score-only rejection sampling: it more effectively suppresses undesirable patterns while promoting beneficial ones, as confirmed by case analyses, and it ultimately improves final test accuracy.

### [83] [SaFeR-Steer: Evolving Multi-Turn MLLMs via Synthetic Bootstrapping and Feedback Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16358)
*Haolong Hu,Hanyu Li,Tiancheng He,Huahui Yi,An Zhang,Qiankun Li,Kun Wang,Yang Liu,Zhigang Zeng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出 SaFeR-Steer 框架，结合分阶段合成数据与导师在环的 GRPO，实现多轮安全对齐；引入 TCSR 机制通过轨迹最小/平均安全度将晚轮失败传播至早轮，提升模型鲁棒性；发布 STEER 多轮多模态安全数据集，涵盖 12,934 条 SFT、2,000 条 RL 和 3,227 条评测对话。实验表明，基于 Qwen2.5-VL-3B/7B 的模型在单轮和多轮基准上均显著提升安全性和帮助性，且失败被延迟至后期，超越单纯缩放效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态大模型在多轮场景中面临安全衰减问题，现有训练数据以单轮为主，无法匹配实际部署中的复杂交互，导致安全对齐存在严重脱节。

Method: 提出 SaFeR-Steer 框架，采用分阶段合成数据进行自举，并引入导师在环的 on-policy GRPO 训练策略；设计 TCSR 机制，利用轨迹最小/平均安全度将晚轮的安全失败回传至早期对话轮次，强化整体安全性。

Result: 在 Qwen2.5-VL-3B/7B 上，单轮安全性和帮助性分别从 48.30/45.86 提升至 81.84/70.77（3B），56.21/60.32 提升至 87.89/77.40（7B）；多轮任务表现从 12.55/27.13 提升至 55.58/70.27（3B），24.66/46.48 提升至 64.89/72.35（7B），失败被有效延后，展现出超越模型规模扩展的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: SaFeR-Steer 有效解决了多轮多模态安全对齐中的现实差距问题，通过动态对抗训练与失败传播机制，显著提升了模型在复杂交互中的安全性与实用性，为未来安全可控的 MLLM 部署提供了新范式。

Abstract: MLLMs are increasingly deployed in multi-turn settings, where attackers can escalate unsafe intent through the evolving visual-text history and exploit long-context safety decay. Yet safety alignment is still dominated by single-turn data and fixed-template dialogues, leaving a mismatch between training and deployment.To bridge this gap, we propose SaFeR-Steer, a progressive multi-turn alignment framework that combines staged synthetic bootstrapping with tutor-in-the-loop GRPO to train a single student under adaptive, on-policy attacks. We also introduce TCSR, which uses trajectory minimum/average safety to propagate late-turn failures to earlier turns.I. Dataset. We release STEER, a multi-turn multimodal safety dataset with STEER-SFT (12,934), STEER-RL (2,000), and STEER-Bench (3,227) dialogues spanning 2~10 turns.II. Experiment. Starting from Qwen2.5-VL-3B/7B, SaFeR-Steer substantially improves Safety/Helpfulness on both single-turn (48.30/45.86 -> 81.84/70.77 for 3B; 56.21/60.32 -> 87.89/77.40 for 7B) and multi-turn benchmarks (12.55/27.13 -> 55.58/70.27 for 3B; 24.66/46.48 -> 64.89/72.35 for 7B), shifting failures to later turns and yielding robustness beyond scaling alone.Codes are available at https://github.com/Ed-Bg/SaFeR-Steer

### [84] [SetFlow: Generating Structured Sets of Representations for Multiple Instance Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16362)
*Nikola Jovišić,Milica Škipina,Vanja Švenda*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出SetFlow，一种直接在表示空间中建模整个MIL数据包（即集合）的生成架构。该方法结合流匹配范式与受Set Transformer启发的设计，能够处理置换不变输入并捕捉包内实例间的交互关系。模型基于类别标签和输入尺度进行条件生成，从而生成语义一致且连贯的表示集合。在大规模乳腺摄影基准测试中，生成样本能准确匹配原始数据分布，并提升下游任务性能；仅使用合成数据训练也表现良好，证明了表示空间生成建模在数据稀缺和隐私敏感任务中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MIL方法在数据稀缺和弱监督场景下受限，尤其在乳腺摄影等应用中，传统增强方法仅作用于实例级别，无法捕捉包内实例间依赖关系，导致生成效果有限。因此需要一种能直接建模整个包结构、捕获内部交互的新方法。

Method: 提出SetFlow，采用流匹配框架与Set Transformer结构相结合，以实现对置换不变输入的建模；通过引入类别标签和输入尺度作为条件，使生成过程具备语义一致性；在表示空间中直接生成完整数据包，保留实例间的上下文关联。

Result: 在乳腺摄影大规模基准上验证，生成样本与真实数据分布高度一致；用于数据增强可提升下游分类性能；仅用合成数据训练即达到竞争性结果，表明该方法在数据稀缺和隐私敏感场景下的潜力。

Conclusion: SetFlow通过在表示空间中直接建模整个MIL包，有效解决了传统方法忽略包内依赖的问题，实现了高质量的生成与增强，在数据稀缺和隐私敏感任务中具有广泛应用前景。

Abstract: Data scarcity and weak supervision continue to limit the performance of machine learning models in many real-world applications, such as mammography, where Multiple Instance Learning (MIL) often offers the best formulation. While recent foundation models provide strong semantic representations out of the box, effective augmentation of such representations of MIL data remains limited, as existing methods operate at the instance level and fail to capture intra-bag dependencies. In this work, we introduce SetFlow, a generative architecture that models entire MIL bags (i.e., sets) directly in the representation space. Our approach leverages the flow matching paradigm combined with a Set Transformer-inspired design, enabling it to handle permutation-invariant inputs while capturing interactions between instances within each bag. The model is conditioned on both class labels and input scale, allowing it to generate coherent and semantically consistent sets of representations. We evaluate SetFlow on a large-scale mammography benchmark using a state-of-the-art MIL-PF classification pipeline. The generated samples are shown to closely match the original data distribution and even improve downstream performance when used for augmentation. Furthermore, training on synthetic data alone shows competitive results, demonstrating the effectiveness of representation-space generative modeling for data-scarce and privacy-sensitive tasks.

</details>


### [85] [Matched-Learning-Rate Analysis of Attention Drift and Transfer Retention in Fine-Tuned CLIP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16410)
*Ruize Xia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过在相同学习率下对比全微调（Full FT）与LoRA，揭示了优化规模与适配方法如何共同影响CLIP模型的注意力漂移和迁移性能。结果显示，在匹配学习率条件下，LoRA相比Full FT显著保留了更强的零样本迁移能力（如EuroSAT上平均达45.13% vs 11.28%的CIFAR-100准确率），且注意力熵保持正向变化，而Full FT随学习率升高出现明显收缩。此外，低学习率下LoRA可能欠拟合，因此仅比较方法平均值会掩盖其实际表现。整体表明，注意力漂移更适合作为表征保留的描述性诊断工具，而非解释迁移行为的因果机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究中，全微调（Full FT）与LoRA的比较常因学习率设定差异而产生混淆，导致对两者在迁移性能与注意力结构变化上的判断失真。本文旨在通过控制学习率，澄清适配方法与优化规模的联合影响，以更准确评估二者在域内准确率与域外迁移能力之间的权衡。

Method: 采用受控的匹配学习率实验设计，在CLIP ViT-B/32上进行80次运行，覆盖四个学习率（$10^{-6}$, $5\times10^{-6}$, $10^{-5}$, $5\times10^{-5}$）和五个随机种子，分别在EuroSAT和Oxford-IIIT Pets数据集上评估注意力漂移、最佳验证准确率及适配器感知的CIFAR-100零样本准确率。同时结合卷积核分析（CKA）、逐块展开（rollout）和像素级注意力图等多维度分析支持结论。

Result: 在匹配学习率条件下，LoRA始终维持较高的注意力熵（熵正向），而Full FT随学习率上升呈现显著收缩。在零样本迁移任务中，LoRA平均优于Full FT：EuroSAT上为45.13% vs 11.28%，Pets上为58.01% vs 8.54%。低学习率下LoRA存在欠拟合问题，因此方法间平均表现可能误导判断。多种分析手段方向一致，支持核心发现。

Conclusion: 在匹配学习率下重新评估表明，传统比较中对Full FT与LoRA的优劣判断需修正；注意力漂移是表征保留的良好描述性指标，但不宜作为解释迁移行为的因果依据。

Abstract: CLIP adaptation can improve in-domain accuracy while degrading out-of-domain transfer, but comparisons between Full Fine-Tuning (Full FT) and LoRA are often confounded by different learning-rate conventions. We study how adaptation method and optimization scale jointly shape attention drift and transfer retention in CLIP using a controlled matched-learning-rate comparison of Full FT and LoRA. The completed matrix contains 80 runs on CLIP ViT-B/32 across EuroSAT and Oxford-IIIT Pets, spanning four shared learning rates ($10^{-6}$, $5{\times}10^{-6}$, $10^{-5}$, $5{\times}10^{-5}$) and five seeds, and evaluates attention-drift metrics, best validation accuracy, and adapter-aware CIFAR-100 zero-shot accuracy. Learning rate strongly modulates structural change: on EuroSAT, Full FT moves from mild entropy broadening at $10^{-6}$ to marked contraction at $5{\times}10^{-5}$, whereas LoRA remains entropy-positive across the full matched grid. At matched learning rates, LoRA preserves substantially more zero-shot transfer than Full FT, averaging $45.13\%$ versus $11.28\%$ CIFAR-100 accuracy on EuroSAT and $58.01\%$ versus $8.54\%$ on Pets. Oxford-IIIT Pets also reveals a regime effect: low-learning-rate LoRA underfits in-domain, so method-only averages can obscure when LoRA becomes competitive. Supporting rollout, patch-to-patch, and CKA analyses are directionally consistent with the controlled matrix. Overall, matched-learning-rate evaluation materially changes the interpretation of Full FT versus LoRA, and attention drift is most useful as a descriptive diagnostic of representation preservation rather than a causal explanation of transfer behavior.

</details>


### [86] [Shifting the Gradient: Understanding How Defensive Training Methods Protect Language Model Integrity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.16423)
*Satchel Grant,Victor Gillioz,Jake Ward,Thomas McGrath*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PPS和IP虽表面相似，但机制不同：PPS通过调整激活梯度来抑制或逆转特质表达，而IP则通过‘解释消除’训练数据中的特质表达，其机制更模糊且扩散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究防御性训练方法PPS与IP在对抗大语言模型习得不良特质时的内在机制差异，特别是它们是否基于相同原理。

Method: 采用行为实验与机制分析相结合的方法，以‘邪恶性’为案例研究，比较两种方法在行为表现与梯度方向上的差异，并通过余弦相似度与损失函数变化进行量化验证。

Result: PPS能有效防御并减少已有特质表达，其机制是沿特定向量轴改变激活梯度；而IP对已有特质模型无效，其梯度更分散，且通过降低预测损失‘解释掉’特质表达，暗示其机制不明确。

Conclusion: PPS与IP并非同质机制，前者具有可解释的梯度调控能力，后者则表现出模糊、扩散的响应模式，提示需进一步探索IP的深层机理。

Abstract: Defensive training methods such as positive preventative steering (PPS) and inoculation prompting (IP) offer surprising results through seemingly similar processes: both add trait-inducing objects to large language models (LLMs) during training, and both defend the LLM against acquiring the trait. The surprising success of these methods comes with the question: how do they work? Are PPS and IP doing the same thing? We provide behavioral and mechanistic comparisons of these two methods using "evilness" as a case-study trait. Our central finding is that PPS and IP achieve their defensive benefits through distinct mechanisms. Behaviorally, we show that neither PPS nor IP operates through a purely associative mechanism; and PPS can both defend against trait acquisition and actively reduce pre-existing expression, whereas IP is ineffective in models that were previously finetuned to express the trait. This behavioral divergence is reflected mechanistically: PPS shifts the activation gradient towards an attenuating direction along the PPS vector axis. When the PPS vector is aligned with a trait-expressing axis, it can reverse the gradient pressure, reducing rather than increasing activation along that axis. In contrast, IP continues to resist a precise mechanistic account. Direct cosine similarity analyses reveal that IP has a characteristically different gradient signature than PPS, and qualitative analyses reveal IP's gradient to be more diffuse. Furthermore, IP reduces the next-token prediction loss on trait-expressing data where PPS need not, consistent with the notion that IP "explains away" the trait-expression in the training data. Taken together, our analyses reveal distinct mechanisms by which each method operates and highlight open questions about IP's mechanistic picture.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究常将非平稳性与分布漂移混淆，忽视了经典时间序列分析中非平稳性作为过程脱离稳定状态的诊断意义，尤其在统计过程控制（SPC）中至关重要。本文旨在厘清这一概念，并探究非平稳性在TSFM嵌入空间中的可检测性。

Method: 通过控制条件下的扰动实验，系统测试不同强度的均值偏移、方差变化和线性趋势，以及由长记忆或近单位根行为引发的持久性非平稳性，评估多种TSFM在嵌入空间中的检测能力。
